PREFACE 

This workbook accompanies Hindi for Non-Hindi Speaking People, a 

. two-in-one monograph that serves both as reference grammar as well as reader 

for beginners. 

The workbook has been designed to cater to the needs of students who 
have already studied the basic structures of Hindi but who still commit some 

. grammatical mistakes and have difficulties in using the language. The book 
| provides plenty of material for written practice in all the principal structures 
_ which appear in the master volume Hindi for Non-Hindi Speaking People. 

| 
| 
| 
| 
| 
| 
| 
| 
| 
| 

It is neither so intended nor necessary for the students to work through 
this book from beginning to end. The contents pages list the underlying key 
structures of the exercises. The students can refer to these contents and 
practise selectively to suit their requirements. 

An answer key is provided at the end for self evaluation and glossaries 
for all the Hindi and English words used in the book are included. 

Vara n asi 
November, 1998 

Kavita Kumar

the intransitive passive construction: 

मेरा संदूक चुरा लिया गया | मेरा संदूक चोरी हो गया | 
इस शहर में एक नया पुल बनाया गया है | 
हमारे मुहल्ले में नई सड़कें डाली गई È | 
आपने घर साफ कर दिया? 

तस्वीर दीवार पर टॉग दी गई है। 

मैंने मेले में सारा सामान बेच दिया। 

धोबी ने कपड़े धो दिए हैं। 

सब दरवाजे खिड़कियाँ बन्द किए जा चुके हैं।

Reflexive pronouns आप 

As reflexive pronoun आप”, आप ही”, आप ही आप?, अपने a’, अपने आप' etc. are 

used to mean by oneself, without anybody's help etc. . 

Their exact meaning depends upon the subject they reflect. 

They remain the same for all three persons,singular as well as plural. 

अपना, अपने, अपनी corresponds to English ‘ones own'. 115 used adjectively and 
| agrees with the number and gender of the noun it modifies. The object in the 
| sentence or a clause belongs to the subject. 
Are all these your own houses? 

| 1. क्या ये सब तुम्हारे अपने मकान हैं? 
He keeps his things carefully. 

वह अपनी चीजें सम्भालकर रखता है | 

यह मेरा अपना फैसला है। This is my own decision.

Base form of the adjective: 

आ - ending adjectives e.g. बड़ा, छोटा etc. 

These are declinable, they take आ, ए, $ ending in accordance With the ny 
and gender of the noun they modify. However, they have no ‘ay’ Or at; |

to qualify the plural nouns in the oblique or vocative cases

ये नए ad हैं। These are new ‘kurtas' 

इन नए eal को सन्दूक में रखो । Keep these new 'Kurtas' in the box. 

Feminine form (नई here) is invariable 
All other adjectives e.g. सुन्दर, भारी, दयालु etc. 

These are indeclinable. They are invariable whatever be the number andge 
of noun they modify. | 

 Comparatives: 

To change the base adjective to comparative, से, से कहीं, से अधिक, से ज्यादा, ऐ | 
से बढ़कर, की अपेक्षा, की तुलना में, में से ete. are used

verb : HNP 143-165 

stative Verb — होना (to be)e.g. राम होशियार है। Ram is clever. 
Change of state verbs — हो जाना, बनना (to become), 
मालूम होना (to become known) 

राम छात्रावास में जाकर होशियार हो गया Ram has become very clever after going to 
है। the hostel. 

स्वाती डॉक्टर बन गई है | Swati has become a doctor. | 
मुझे सब मालूम हो गया है। Everything has become known to me. 

Action verbs — करना (do), खाना (eat), दौड़ना (run), पढ़ना (read) etc. 
Volitional verbs — these denote deliberate actions. 
e.g. फाड़ना (to tear ), बनाना (to make), तोड़ना (to break) 

उसने मेरा कुर्ता फाड़ा। He tore my ‘Kurta’. 
बच्चे' ने गमला तोडा The child broke the flowerpot. 
राम ने नया मकान बनाया है। Ram has built a new house. 

Non-volitional verbs — These denote accidental happening or the existing state 
of things. e.g. फटना (to be torn) , बनना (to be made), दूटना (to be broken) 

मेरा कुर्ता फट गया | My ‘Kurta’ got torn. | 
गमला टूटा है | The flowerpot is broken. 
रानी का नया मकान बन गया है | Rani's new house has been built. 

Transitive verbs — These are verbs that have an accusative object and that 

answer the question ‘what'? 

` राम चावल खाता है। Ram eats rice. 
subj. d.o. v.t. 

Question : राम क्या खाता है? What does Ram eat? 
Answer : चावल Rice [accusative (direct) object. ] 

Double transitive verbs — These have two objects, an accusative (direct) object 
and a dative (indirect) object. 

9. राम पिता जी को पत्र लिखता है। Ram writes a letter to father.

Use of suffix वाला” | HNP 97-100 

The suffix वाला' frequently used in Hindi denotes various things with different kinds of 
words. Colloquially, it is used chiefly in association with nouns, adjectives, adverbs 
and the oblique form of the infinitive. It is an adjectival suffix and hence subject to 

change like any other adjective following the rule pertaining to आ', ‘ए’, ‘ई’ form. Sg., 
m. pl., f. sg. and pl., respectively. 

[(v.r. + ने) + वाला ] can be used to convey two things 
itis equivalent to the English suffix 'er; the one who does something 

itis used to convey that something is about to/expected to happen. 
Noun + वाला indicates proprietorship, cost or value, what something is made of, 

Seller of an article etc. 
Demonstrative pronouns + वाला, used to point to a particular person or thing. 

Adjective + वाला, वाले, वाली, to single out one in a group. 

ce. it indic ition 
When added to an adverb or the name of a place; It indicates posit

| or residence.

The possessive case — use of का, के, की HNP 110 

The possessive form has the case endings का, के, की 

These endings precede the object possessed. 
They agree with the number and gender of the object possessed and not with ne 
number and gender of the possessor.

।. मुझे आकाश में कुछ चिड़ियाँ उड़ती हुई 2. अर्जुन को सिर्फ मछली की आँख दिखाई दे 
दिखाई दे रही E रही थी। 
3. कुछ नावें हमारी ओर आती हुई दिखाई 4. हमें तट की ओर बढ़ती हुई समुद्री लहरे 
दे रही थीं। दिखाई दे रही थीं | 
Key 58 
1. हमें पड़ोस से ऊंची ऊँची आवाजें सुनाई 2. क्या आपको कुछ सुनाई दे रहा है? 
दे रही थीं। 
3. मुझे रात-दिन मंदिर की घंटियों और 4. अचानक उसे किसीके पैरों की आहट सुनाई 
मस्जिद की नमाजों की आवाजें सुनाई देती हैं । दी। | 
Ex. 59 

1. सविता अपनी माता जी जैसी लगती है। 

2. गणित = बहुत कठिन लगता है। 

3. मुझे देहात का जीवन अच्छा लगता है। 

4. छोटे बच्चों को दिन में कई बार भूख लगती है। 

5. आजकल यहाँ दो कमरे का मकान किराए पर लेने के लिए एक महीने के दो हजार रुपए लगते 
हैं | 

6. यहाँ से रेलगाड़ी से बम्बई पहुँचने में कितने घण्टे लगते हैं। 
7. शनिवार को हमारे इलाके में सब्जी बाजार लगता है। 

8. अनिल तुम्हारा कौन लगता है!

This workbook has been specially designed as a self-study or classroom companion 
volume to Hindi for Non-Hindi Speaking People. The exercises included here reinforce 
the key grammar points, offer the learners enough practice material to get to grips 
with various language structures and enable them to communicate effectively and 

confidently in written and spoken Hindi. 

Its special features are: 

e Hindi grammar exercises, fully cross referenced to Hindi for Non-Hindi Speaking 
People. 

e Translation practice from English to Hindi. 

e Vocabulary and expressions in active use for common everyday situations. 
e Hindi grammar at a glance for ready reference. 

e Complete answer key to all exercises. 

e Comprehensive glossaries in Hindi and English. 

ISBN 81-7167-333-3
